< review>
Amazing and great place highly recommend, team does a great job very friendly, professional and very passionate to the the task given. I came in with a Honda Civic 2015(I did not take any before pics üòì) but i can describe so I just got the car, interior was disgusting smelled horrible like cigarettes and old mj  and somethin else (summer around the corner )  carpet had like gunk build up dirt build up one had like a baking soda looking stain. Pet hair, Dash board was  layered with dust like you can see the brown on it. Seats stained dirty. Oh and the soda holder and door handle was treated as an ash tray. The trunk was gross like old brown liquid in it where spare wheel was sandy dirty trunk. Now for the exterior Rims looked bland the exterior of the car looked bland dirty spotty.
Andres gave me options what he can offer not upselling me explained what he can do and went over about exterior, from simple wash, waxing, or ceramic to coat the car
I asked them to give me the top notch stuff make it new looking like if they were selling the car to me. So went with shampooing and detail clean inside car as well as ceramic I was quoted almost $300 I was completely ok with it. Since it was disgusting.

These guys really put in the work and it shows. I drop off the car 9am got it back at 5pm (reasonable since it was a really disgusting car and they needed to multitask with easy job cars, i did not mind)
I was super excited to see the car like new I gave them about  20% tip. Thats how happy I was. Exterior looks amazing like a mirror.
In a photo I add you can see a palm tree reflected. Oh and it smelled great.
I will be taking my other car here and use this place for deep cleaning for my cars.</review>

< Text>
The most friendly, clean, well stocked, and knowledgeable location within this area/region by far! The location on the exterior may be misleading without your typical neon lights and large name displays, though once inside that is truly where the magic begins. From the non-extensive paper to the kind and curious doorman, the first time patient check was in my opinion flawless, non discriminatory, and professional.
Once inside not sure who may provide you service but the gentleman by the name of Joseph helped in assisting me with my visit. The quality, layout, and choice selection inside  this dispensary was immaculate, and that may be an under statement. I was not rushed or manipulated in any way when making my selections which is a huge relief when you're a bit of a stickler and/or very sensitive to your preferencesite.
Lastly i'd like to add that the pricing was the peak point ending my experience on an incredible high note. I would recommend this dispensary to both the young and older community of patients being that this location can easily accommodate any type of patient. Thank you "The Crop" and keep doing what you're doing.....Ashton....üòä</Text>

<Review>It's been ages since I've gone out for omakase it seems. However, my friend Kurt hit me up to try a new spot. Such great timing! In addition to that, a recent article from OC Weekly came out listing the top 10 sushi spots, so this dinner was destined to happen one way or another. As we went back and forth on the prime meet up spot, we settled on Hamamori for its convenience and the fact that neither of us have been.

Arrived on location at 6p to a slow evening, but it was nice to have the bar to ourselves. As we reviewed the menu, we started the evening with a taste of sake since we were indecisive on which to choose from. We sampled a choice of sweet or dry and settled on the dry to pair with our meal. To go with the ambiance, each pour is served in a champagne flute instead of the usual you see, so it sets the tone for a fancy meal ahead, in which I was eager to taste.

We inquired about omakase and the chef began the meal. With each plating, we were served two pieces at a time. The opening sequence was albacore with crispy onions and golden eye snapper. The chef made it a note to request no soy sauce as each was seasoned individually and made to complement the fish.

We totaled at 18 pieces:
Sea bream and Blackthroat Seaperch.
Wagyu Beef/Foie Gras and Lobster/Miso
Salmon/Pineapple and Sweet Live Shrimp/Caviar/Lemon Zest
Halibut/Foie Gras and King Scallop
Bluefin Tuna/Bleu Cheese/Seaweed Sauce and Seared Yellowtail/Jalapeno
O Toro and Shima Aji
Eel/Foie Gras/Orange Zest
Halibut Tempura Handroll
Sea Urchin and Yellowtail

To conclude, the meal was spectacular and just what I was craving for. I could go for a little less foie gras since I'm not superbly wow'd by it, but it did complement most of the pairings that evening. However, I'm just a bit skeptical on pricing since I feel I could get something on par for a third of the price less. Still, it was a great meal nonetheless and I would return for a fancy meal every once in awhile, but it's not my go-to sushi fix.< /Review><pics>None< /pics><Resp>None<//Resp>< Gmap_id>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
San Diego, inexpensive dinner and/or drinks cruise on Mission Bay.  Always lots a fun for a short round trip cruise.  Very friendly staff.  Boats are getting a bit older but still very nice.  Indoor seating for chilly nights or outdoor, top deck seating is a great option. First come, first serve.  Have to get there early, but nice hanging out at the bay.  Line getting on moves quickly.  Always a good size crowd, especially because a few hotels give free vouchers like the catamaran.  Worth the time when down by Mission Bay.< /review>

<pictures>None</pictures>< Rating>
2< /Rating>
< text>
While waiting for the cruise, it is nice to relax on the cabana lounge chairs on the beach. No reservation needed, first come first serve.

For hotel guest, the ride is FREE.

The Service: So so.... the cruise leaves every hour, you can stay as long as you want. Unfortunately, many passengers love it so much and they wouldn't get off the cruise. At the end, they could not board the passengers waiting at the pier (they have specific capacity). We had to wait for one more hour & pray that there would have enough room for us..... :(

The Bar: Limited choices of cocktail.

The first level of the cruise is not open. The second level of the cruise is the bar & dance floor. Very small dance floor.... super crowded. They put chairs on two sides of the dance floor. Good music, however, no room to dance. The third level of the cruise is the open deck. 9 benches for seating. It is also the "smoking area".

It is about 45 minutes of ride. Unfortunately, not much to see at the Mission Bay.<//text>

<Time>1468446429911<//Time><Rate>5< /Rate><Text>(Translated by Google) Wawona, located at the southern entrance to Yosemite, was originally an Indian settlement. In 1865, Galen Clark built a Clark Station in the name of his own name, and visitors to the Yosemite Valley could spend the night here. In 1864, the Mariposa Grove, consisting of the Yosemite Valley and the huge redwoods, was officially protected by the Yosemite Grant. Clark was nominated as the first director of Yosemite (guardian). In 1875, the Wawona Highway was opened to traffic, and the Washburn brothers acquired the land. They built the Wawona Lodge and are still open until now.
In Wawona, visitors can learn about the development of Yosemite and the people involved. Showcase historic pioneering houses and carriages at the Pioneer Yosemite History Center

<rate>3<//rate>< text>
Not the greatest Dog park, probably worth the drive to go to either Highland park or the Griffith park dog park if you've got the time. Lots of aggressive dogs here and even though it is quite large it often feels overly crowded. Lots of owners not paying attention to their dogs, lots of un-neutered dogs. I've seen huge dog fights here because people bring dogs in heat or just aggressive, untrained dogs. Its usually super dusty and muddy and we always have to bathe our dog after coming here. Unfortunately its the closest one to us so we go somewhat often, but when time allows we always go elsewhere.</text>

<rating>3< /rating>< userid>
110859488917607711058< /userid>
<username>Dawn Ailetcher</username>< Time>
1581483547055</Time>
<response>None</response>< Review>
On the plus side, they have a designated small dog side that is separate from the big dog side. There is an easily accessible watering area. They have desiganted entrance and exit gates that are double gated so that dogs are less likely to escape.
The people who hang out at this park are awesome. Fun loving, good spirited, dog people. They not only enjoy the company of dogs, but the humans who accompany them also. Introduce yourself, have a great conversation, and watch your dogs play together.
There are a few nice seating areas. A couple of fixed picnic benches, a bench, and some plastic chairs you can move around.
Stuff that's good to know for you and your dogs..
There is not much shade, so if you're visiting on a hot, sunny day, bring a hat and some sunscreen.
There is not much grass, so it cn be dusty on a windy day. Bring the puppy wipes to keep your car free of dusty dog paw prints.
If you're driving to the park, parking can be tough. Be prepared to loop a couple of times to find a spot. If you're bringing an older dog, there are hills on the walk to the park thy may be difficult for those with hip and or knee problems.</Review>
